  padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt;height:15.0pt"><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom:0in;line-height:normal"><span lang="EN-SG" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">zahara_osman@moe.edu.sg</span><span style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;mso-fareast-font-family:

  mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-bidi-language:TA"></span></p></td></tr></tbody></table>
